        $(document).ready(function () {
            $('#cssmenu ul ul li:odd').addClass('odd');
            $('#cssmenu ul ul li:even').addClass('even');
            $('#cssmenu > ul > li > a').click(function () {
                $('#cssmenu li').removeClass('active');
                $(this).closest('li').addClass('active');
                var checkElement = $(this).next();
                if ((checkElement.is('ul')) && (checkElement.is(':visible'))) {
                    $(this).closest('li').removeClass('active');
                    checkElement.slideUp('normal');
                }
                if ((checkElement.is('ul')) && (!checkElement.is(':visible'))) {
                    $('#cssmenu ul ul:visible').slideUp('normal');
                    checkElement.slideDown('normal');
                }
                if ($(this).closest('li').find('ul').children().length == 0) {
                    return true;
                } else {
                    return false;
                }
            });
        });
    </script>

	function showSearchResultDomain(state, type){
		
		var seperator = seperatorVal;
		if(state == 1){
			//$('#searchResult').html('');
			$('#counterVal').html(0);
			$('#finalSearchResult').html('');
			counter = 0;
		}
		if(type == 'inner'){
			tempSearchStr = '';
		}

		if($('#chkRequirePr').prop("checked") == true){
		    counter++;
			if(tempSearchStr!=''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
			}
			tempSearchStr += ' Has Page Rank ';
		}
/*
                if($('#chkShowFakePr').prop("checked") == true){
		    counter++;
			if(tempSearchStr!=''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
			}
			tempSearchStr += ' Hide Fake PR ';
		}
*/
		if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitPageRank").val()) != 0 && Math.round($("#upperLimitPageRank").val()) != 0){
			counter++;
			if(tempSearchStr!=''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
			}
			tempSearchStr += 'Page Rank from '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitPageRank").val())) +' to '+ number_format(Math.round($("#upperLimitPageRank").val()));
		}
		else{
			if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitPageRank").val()) != 0){
				counter++;
				tempSearchStr += 'Page Rank more than '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitPageRank").val()));
			}
			else if(Math.round($("#upperLimitPageRank").val()) != 0){
				counter++;
				tempSearchStr += 'Page Rank less than '+ number_format(Math.round($("#upperLimitPageRank").val()));
			}
		}


		if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitWhoIsAge").val()) != 0 && Math.round($("#upperLimitWhoIsAge").val()) != 0){

				$('#counterVal').html(counter);

				//$('#searchResult').html("<b id='counterValBTag'><span id='counterVal'>"+counter+"</span> filters enabled.</b><a href='javascript:void(0)' onClick='showAllFilter()'>Show all filters.</a> <a href='javascript:void(0)' onClick='ToggleSearchPanel()' id='aLinkSearch'>Show search screen.</a> <span id='finalSearchResult' style='display:none'>"+tempSearchStr+"</span>");

<script type="text/javascript">
	jQuery(function($) 
	{
		$('#lowerLimitAlexaRank').ace_spinner({min:0, max:99999999, value:'', step:1, btn_up_class:'btn-info' , btn_down_class:'btn-info', speed:'fast'});
		$('#upperLimitAlexaRank').ace_spinner({min:0, max:99999999, value:'', step:1, btn_up_class:'btn-info' , btn_down_class:'btn-info', speed:'fast'});
		$('#lowerLimitAlexaRankReach').ace_spinner({min:0, max:99999999, value:'', step:1, btn_up_class:'btn-info' , btn_down_class:'btn-info', speed:'fast'});
		$('#upperLimitAlexaRankReach').ace_spinner({min:0, max:99999999, value:'', step:1, btn_up_class:'btn-info' , btn_down_class:'btn-info', speed:'fast'});
		$('#lowerLimitAlexaRankDelta').ace_spinner({min:0, max:99999, value:'', step:1, btn_up_class:'btn-info' , btn_down_class:'btn-info', speed:'fast'});
		$('#upperLimitAlexaRankDelta').ace_spinner({min:0, max:99999, value:'', step:1, btn_up_class:'btn-info' , btn_down_class:'btn-info', speed:'fast'});
		$('#lowerLimitAlexaLinks').ace_spinner({min:0, max:99999, value:'', step:1, btn_up_class:'btn-info' , btn_down_class:'btn-info', speed:'fast'});
		$('#upperLimitAlexaLinks').ace_spinner({min:0, max:99999, value:'', step:1, btn_up_class:'btn-info' , btn_down_class:'btn-info', speed:'fast'});
		$('#lowerLimitAlexaCountryRank').ace_spinner({min:0, max:99999999, value:'', step:1, btn_up_class:'btn-info' , btn_down_class:'btn-info', speed:'fast'});
		$('#upperLimitAlexaCountryRank').ace_spinner({min:0, max:99999999, value:'', step:1, btn_up_class:'btn-info' , btn_down_class:'btn-info', speed:'fast'});

	})

	function showSearchResultAlexaMetrics(type){
		var seperator = '';
		if(jQuery('#counterVal').html() != '0'){
			if(jQuery('#counterVal').html() != ''){
				var counter1 = eval(jQuery('#counterVal').html());
			}

			if(jQuery('#finalSearchResult').html() != ''){
				var seperator = seperatorVal;
				var tempSearchStr = jQuery('#finalSearchResult').html();
			}
		}
		else{
			var seperator = seperatorVal;
			var counter1 = counter;
			var tempSearchStr = '';
		}
		if(type == 'inner'){
			tempSearchStr = '';
		}
		
		if($('#chkRequireAlexaRank').prop("checked") == true){
		    counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr!=''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
			}
			tempSearchStr += ' Has Alexa Rank ';
		}
		
		if($('#chkHideFakeAr').prop("checked") == true){
		    counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr!=''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
			}
			tempSearchStr += ' Hide Fake Alexa Ranks ';
		}

		if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitAlexaRank").val()) != 0 && Math.round($("#upperLimitAlexaRank").val()) != 0){
			counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
			}
			tempSearchStr += 'Alexa Rank from '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitAlexaRank").val())) +' to '+ number_format(Math.round($("#upperLimitAlexaRank").val()));
		}
		else{
			if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitAlexaRank").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'Alexa Rank more than '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitAlexaRank").val()));
			}
			else if(Math.round($("#upperLimitAlexaRank").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'Alexa Rank less than '+ number_format(Math.round($("#upperLimitAlexaRank").val()));
			}
		}

		if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitAlexaRankReach").val()) != 0 && Math.round($("#upperLimitAlexaRankReach").val()) != 0){
			counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
			}
			tempSearchStr += 'Alexa Rank Reach from '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitAlexaRankReach").val())) +' to '+ number_format(Math.round($("#upperLimitAlexaRankReach").val()));
		}
		else{
			if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitAlexaRankReach").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'Alexa Rank Reach more than '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitAlexaRankReach").val()));
			}
			else if(Math.round($("#upperLimitAlexaRankReach").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'Alexa Rank Reach less than '+ number_format(Math.round($("#upperLimitAlexaRankReach").val()));
			}
		}

		if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitAlexaRankDelta").val()) != 0 && Math.round($("#upperLimitAlexaRankDelta").val()) != 0){
			counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
			}
			tempSearchStr += 'Alexa Rank Delta from '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitAlexaRankDelta").val())) +' to '+ number_format(Math.round($("#upperLimitAlexaRankDelta").val()));
		}
		else{
			if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitAlexaRankDelta").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'Alexa Rank Delta more than '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitAlexaRankDelta").val()));
			}
			else if(Math.round($("#upperLimitAlexaRankDelta").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'Alexa Rank Delta less than '+ number_format(Math.round($("#upperLimitAlexaRankDelta").val()));
			}
		}

		if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitAlexaLinks").val()) != 0 && Math.round($("#upperLimitAlexaLinks").val()) != 0){
			counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
			}
			tempSearchStr += 'Alexa Links from '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitAlexaLinks").val())) +' to '+ number_format(Math.round($("#upperLimitAlexaLinks").val()));
		}
		else{
			if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitAlexaLinks").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'Alexa Links more than '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitAlexaLinks").val()));
			}
			else if(Math.round($("#upperLimitAlexaLinks").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'Alexa Links less than '+ number_format(Math.round($("#upperLimitAlexaLinks").val()));
			}
		}

		if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitAlexaCountryRank").val()) != 0 && Math.round($("#upperLimitAlexaCountryRank").val()) != 0){
			counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
			}
			tempSearchStr += 'Alexa Country Rank from '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitAlexaCountryRank").val())) +' to '+ number_format(Math.round($("#upperLimitAlexaCountryRank").val()));
		}
		else{
			if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitAlexaCountryRank").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'Alexa Country Rank more than '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitAlexaCountryRank").val()));
			}
			else if(Math.round($("#upperLimitAlexaCountryRank").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'Alexa Country Rank less than '+ number_format(Math.round($("#upperLimitAlexaCountryRank").val()));
			}
		}

		if(type == 'inner'){
			return tempSearchStr;
		}
		else{
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				$('#counterVal').html('');
				$('#finalSearchResult').html('');
				$('#counterVal').html(counter1);
				$('#finalSearchResult').html(tempSearchStr);
				//$('#searchResult').html('');
				//$('#searchResult').html("<b id='counterValBTag'><span id='counterVal'>"+counter1+"</span> filters enabled.</b><a href='javascript:void(0)' onClick='showAllFilter()'>Show all filters.</a> <a href='javascript:void(0)' onClick='ToggleSearchPanel()' id='aLinkSearch'>Show search screen</a> <span id='finalSearchResult' style='display:none'>"+tempSearchStr+"</span>");
				/*if(tempSearchStr.length > maxCharacterDisplay){
					$('#searchResult').html("<a data-rel='tooltip' data-placement='bottom' style='color:#393939;text-decoration:none;' href='javascript:void(0)' class='tooltip-info' title='"+tempSearchStr.replace(/(<([^>]+)>)/ig,"")+"'><b><span id='counterVal'>"+counter+"</span> filters enabled</b>: Showing domains with <span id='finalSearchResult' style='display:none;'>"+tempSearchStr+"</span>"+tempSearchStr.substring(0, maxCharacterDisplay)+"...</a>");
				}
				else{
					$('#searchResult').html("<a data-rel='tooltip' data-placement='bottom' style='color:#393939;text-decoration:none;' href='javascript:void(0)' class='tooltip-info'><b><span id='counterVal'>"+counter+"</span> filters enabled</b>: Showing domains with <span id='finalSearchResult' style='display:none'>"+tempSearchStr+"</span>"+tempSearchStr+"</a>");	
				}*/
			}
		}
	}
</script>

	function showSearchResultMozMetrics(type){
		
		if(jQuery('#searchResult').html() != ''){
			if(jQuery('#counterVal').html() != ''){
				var counter1 = eval(jQuery('#counterVal').html());
			}

			if(jQuery('#finalSearchResult').html() != ''){
				var seperator = seperatorVal;
				var tempSearchStr = jQuery('#finalSearchResult').html();
			}
		}
		else{
			var seperator = seperatorVal;
			var counter1 = counter;
			var tempSearchStr = '';
		}
		if(type == 'inner'){
			tempSearchStr = '';
		}
		


		if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitDomainAuthority").val()) != 0 && Math.round($("#upperLimitDomainAuthority").val()) != 0){
			counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';	
			}
			tempSearchStr += 'Domain Authority from '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitDomainAuthority").val())) +' to '+ number_format(Math.round($("#upperLimitDomainAuthority").val()));
		}
		else{
			if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitDomainAuthority").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';	
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'Domain Authority more than '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitDomainAuthority").val()));
			}
			else if(Math.round($("#upperLimitDomainAuthority").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';	
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'Domain Authority less than '+ number_format(Math.round($("#upperLimitDomainAuthority").val()));
			}
		}

		if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitPageAuthority").val()) != 0 && Math.round($("#upperLimitPageAuthority").val()) != 0){
			counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';	
			}
			tempSearchStr += 'Page Authority from '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitPageAuthority").val())) +' to '+ number_format(Math.round($("#upperLimitPageAuthority").val()));
		}
		else{
			if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitPageAuthority").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';	
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'Page Authority more than '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitPageAuthority").val()));
			}
			else if(Math.round($("#upperLimitPageAuthority").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';

			}
		}


		if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitMozDomains").val()) != 0 && Math.round($("#upperLimitMozDomains").val()) != 0){
			counter1++;

				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';	
			}
			tempSearchStr += 'Referring Domains from '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitMozDomains").val())) +' to '+ number_format(Math.round($("#upperLimitMozDomains").val()));
		}
		else{
			if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitMozDomains").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';	
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'Referring Domains more than '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitMozDomains").val()));
			}
			else if(Math.round($("#upperLimitMozDomains").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';	
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'Referring Domains less than '+ number_format(Math.round($("#upperLimitMozDomains").val()));
			}
		}

		if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitMozSubDomainDomains").val()) != '' && Math.round($("#upperLimitMozSubDomainDomains").val()) != ''){
			counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';	
			}
			tempSearchStr += 'Referring Domains (www) from '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitMozSubDomainDomains").val())) +' to '+ number_format(Math.round($("#upperLimitMozSubDomainDomains").val()));
		}
		else{
			if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitMozSubDomainDomains").val()) != ''){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';	
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'Referring Domains (www) more than '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitMozSubDomainDomains").val()));
			}
			else if(Math.round($("#upperLimitMozSubDomainDomains").val()) != ''){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';	
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'Referring Domains (www) less than '+ number_format(Math.round($("#upperLimitMozSubDomainDomains").val()));
			}
		}

		if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitMozJuiceLinks").val()) != 0 && Math.round($("#upperLimitMozJuiceLinks").val()) != 0){

			}
			tempSearchStr += 'Equity Links from '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitMozJuiceLinks").val())) +' to '+ number_format(Math.round($("#upperLimitMozJuiceLinks").val()));

			}
		}

		if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitMozSpamScore").val()) != 0 && Math.round($("#upperLimitMozSpamScore").val()) != 0){
			counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';	
			}
			tempSearchStr += 'Spam Score from '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitMozSpamScore").val())) +' to '+ number_format(Math.round($("#upperLimitMozSpamScore").val()));
		}
		else{
			if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitMozSpamScore").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';	
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'Spam Score more than '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitMozSpamScore").val()));
			}
			else if(Math.round($("#upperLimitMozSpamScore").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';	
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'Spam Score less than '+ number_format(Math.round($("#upperLimitMozSpamScore").val()));
			}
		}

		if(type == 'inner'){
			return tempSearchStr;
		}
		else{
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				$('#counterVal').html('');
				$('#finalSearchResult').html('');
				$('#counterVal').html(counter1);
				$('#finalSearchResult').html(tempSearchStr);
				//$('#searchResult').html('');
				//$('#searchResult').html("<b id='counterValBTag'><span id='counterVal'>"+counter1+"</span> filters enabled.</b> <a href='javascript:void(0)' onClick='showAllFilter()'>Show all filters.</a> <a href='javascript:void(0)' onClick='ToggleSearchPanel()' id='aLinkSearch'>Show search screen</a> <span id='finalSearchResult' style='display:none'>"+tempSearchStr+"</span>");
				/*if(tempSearchStr.length > maxCharacterDisplay){
					$('#searchResult').html("<a data-rel='tooltip' data-placement='bottom' style='color:#393939;text-decoration:none;' href='javascript:void(0)' class='tooltip-info' title='"+tempSearchStr.replace(/(<([^>]+)>)/ig,"")+"'><b><span id='counterVal'>"+counter+"</span> filters enabled</b>: Showing domains with <span id='finalSearchResult' style='display:none;'>"+tempSearchStr+"</span>"+tempSearchStr.substring(0, maxCharacterDisplay)+"...</a>");
				}
				else{
					$('#searchResult').html("<a data-rel='tooltip' data-placement='bottom' style='color:#393939;text-decoration:none;' href='javascript:void(0)' class='tooltip-info'><b><span id='counterVal'>"+counter+"</span> filters enabled</b>: Showing domains with <span id='finalSearchResult' style='display:none'>"+tempSearchStr+"</span>"+tempSearchStr+"</a>");	
				}*/
			}
		}
	}
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
	jQuery(function($) 
	{
		$('#lowerLimitSEMrushRank').ace_spinner({min:0, max:99999999, value:'', step:1, btn_up_class:'btn-info' , btn_down_class:'btn-info', speed:'fast'});
		$('#upperLimitSEMrushRank').ace_spinner({min:0, max:99999999, value:'', step:1, btn_up_class:'btn-info' , btn_down_class:'btn-info', speed:'fast'});
		$('#lowerLimitSEMrushTraffic').ace_spinner({min:0, max:99999999, value:'', step:1, btn_up_class:'btn-info' , btn_down_class:'btn-info', speed:'fast'});
		$('#upperLimitSEMrushTraffic').ace_spinner({min:0, max:99999999, value:'', step:1, btn_up_class:'btn-info' , btn_down_class:'btn-info', speed:'fast'});
		$('#lowerLimitSEMrushKeywords').ace_spinner({min:0, max:99999, value:'', step:1, btn_up_class:'btn-info' , btn_down_class:'btn-info', speed:'fast'});
		$('#upperLimitSEMrushKeywords').ace_spinner({min:0, max:99999, value:'', step:1, btn_up_class:'btn-info' , btn_down_class:'btn-info', speed:'fast'});
		$('#lowerLimitSEMrushCost').ace_spinner({min:0, max:99999, value:'', step:1, btn_up_class:'btn-info' , btn_down_class:'btn-info', speed:'fast'});
		$('#upperLimitSEMrushCost').ace_spinner({min:0, max:99999, value:'', step:1, btn_up_class:'btn-info' , btn_down_class:'btn-info', speed:'fast'});
	})

	function showSearchResultSemRushMetrics(type){
		var seperator = '';
		if(jQuery('#counterVal').html() != '0'){
			if(jQuery('#counterVal').html() != ''){
				var counter1 = eval(jQuery('#counterVal').html());
			}

			if(jQuery('#finalSearchResult').html() != ''){
				var seperator = seperatorVal;
				var tempSearchStr = jQuery('#finalSearchResult').html();
			}
		}
		else{
			var seperator = seperatorVal;
			var counter1 = counter;
			var tempSearchStr = '';
		}
		if(type == 'inner'){
			tempSearchStr = '';
		}

		if($('#chkRequireSEMRushRank').prop("checked") == true){
		    counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr!=''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
			}
			tempSearchStr += ' Has SEMrush Rank ';
		}

		if($('#chkRequireSEMRushKeywords').prop("checked") == true){
		    counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr!=''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
			}
			tempSearchStr += ' SEMRush Keywords > 0';
		}

		if($('#chkRequireSEMRushTraffic').prop("checked") == true){
		    counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr!=''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
			}
			tempSearchStr += ' SEMRush Traffic > 0';
		}
		
		if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitSEMrushRank").val()) != 0 && Math.round($("#upperLimitSEMrushRank").val()) != 0){
			counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
			}
			tempSearchStr += 'SEMrush Rank from '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitSEMrushRank").val())) +' to '+ number_format(Math.round($("#upperLimitSEMrushRank").val()));
		}
		else{
			if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitSEMrushRank").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'SEMrush Rank more than '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitSEMrushRank").val()));
			}
			else if(Math.round($("#upperLimitSEMrushRank").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'SEMrush Rank less than'+ number_format(Math.round($("#upperLimitSEMrushRank").val()));
			}
		}

		if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitSEMrushTraffic").val()) != 0 && Math.round($("#upperLimitSEMrushTraffic").val()) != 0){
			counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
			}
			tempSearchStr += 'SEMrush Traffic from '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitSEMrushTraffic").val())) +' to '+ number_format(Math.round($("#upperLimitSEMrushTraffic").val()));
		}
		else{
			if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitSEMrushTraffic").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'SEMrush Traffic more than '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitSEMrushTraffic").val()));
			}
			else if(Math.round($("#upperLimitSEMrushTraffic").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'SEMrush Traffic less than '+ number_format(Math.round($("#upperLimitSEMrushTraffic").val()));
			}
		}

		if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitSEMrushKeywords").val()) != 0 && Math.round($("#upperLimitSEMrushKeywords").val()) != 0){
			counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
			}
			tempSearchStr += 'SEMrush Keywords from '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitSEMrushKeywords").val())) +' to '+ number_format(Math.round($("#upperLimitSEMrushKeywords").val()));
		}
		else{
			if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitSEMrushKeywords").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'SEMrush Keywords more than '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitSEMrushKeywords").val()));
			}
			else if(Math.round($("#upperLimitSEMrushKeywords").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'SEMrush Keywords less than '+ number_format(Math.round($("#upperLimitSEMrushKeywords").val()));
			}
		}

		if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitSEMrushCost").val()) != 0 && Math.round($("#upperLimitSEMrushCost").val()) != 0){
			counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
			}
			tempSearchStr += 'SEMrush Cost from '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitSEMrushCost").val())) +' to '+ number_format(Math.round($("#upperLimitSEMrushCost").val()));
		}
		else{
			if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitSEMrushCost").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'SEMrush Cost more than '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitSEMrushCost").val()));
			}
			else if(Math.round($("#upperLimitSEMrushCost").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'SEMrush Cost less than '+ Mnumber_format(ath.round($("#upperLimitSEMrushCost").val()));
			}
		}

		if(type == 'inner'){
			return tempSearchStr;
		}
		else{
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				$('#counterVal').html('');
				$('#finalSearchResult').html('');
				$('#counterVal').html(counter1);
				$('#finalSearchResult').html(tempSearchStr);
				//$('#searchResult').html('');

					$('#searchResult').html("<a data-rel='tooltip' data-placement='bottom' style='color:#393939;text-decoration:none;' href='javascript:void(0)' class='tooltip-info' title='"+tempSearchStr.replace(/(<([^>]+)>)/ig,"")+"'><b><span id='counterVal'>"+counter+"</span> filters enabled</b>: Showing domains with <span id='finalSearchResult' style='display:none;'>"+tempSearchStr+"</span>"+tempSearchStr.substring(0, maxCharacterDisplay)+"...</a>");
				}
				else{

<script language="javascript">
function SelectAuctionTypes(mode)
{
	if(mode == 'all')
	{
		var checkAllAuctions = true;
	}
	else
	if(mode == 'none')
	{
		var checkAllAuctions = false;
	}
	else
	{
		return;
	}
	$('input[name=chkSaleTypeAuctions]').attr('checked', checkAllAuctions);
	$('input[name=chkSaleTypeBuyNow]').attr('checked', checkAllAuctions);	
	$('input[name=chkSaleTypeCloseout]').attr('checked', checkAllAuctions);
	$('input[name=chkSaleTypePending]').attr('checked', checkAllAuctions);
	$('input[name=chkSaleTypeOffer]').attr('checked', checkAllAuctions);
	$('input[name=chkBargainBin]').attr('checked', checkAllAuctions);
}

function showSearchResultAuctionTypes(type){
	var totalCheckedValAuctionType = 6;
	var checkboxCounterAuctionType = 0;
	
	if($('#chkSaleTypeAuctions').prop("checked") == true){
	    checkboxCounterAuctionType++;
	}
	if($('#chkSaleTypeBuyNow').prop("checked") == true){
	    checkboxCounterAuctionType++;
	}
	if($('#chkSaleTypeCloseout').prop("checked") == true){
	    checkboxCounterAuctionType++;
	}
	if($('#chkSaleTypePending').prop("checked") == true){
	    checkboxCounterAuctionType++;
	}
	if($('#chkSaleTypeOffer').prop("checked") == true){
	    checkboxCounterAuctionType++;
	}
	if($('#chkBargainBin').prop("checked") == true){
	    checkboxCounterAuctionType++;
	}

	if(checkboxCounterAuctionType <= totalCheckedValAuctionType-1){
		var seperator = '';
		if(jQuery('#searchResult').html() != ''){
			if(jQuery('#counterVal').html() != ''){
				var counter1 = eval(jQuery('#counterVal').html());
			}

			if(jQuery('#finalSearchResult').html() != ''){
				var seperator = seperatorVal;
				var tempSearchStr = jQuery('#finalSearchResult').html();
			}
		}
		else{
			var seperator = seperatorVal;
			var counter1 = counter;
			var tempSearchStr = '';
		}
		if(type == 'inner'){
			tempSearchStr = '';
			var seperator = 'Or';
		}
		
		var extraString = '';

		if($('#chkSaleTypeAuctions').prop("checked") == true){
		    counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
			}
			tempSearchStr += extraString+' Auctions';
			extraString = '';
		}
		if($('#chkSaleTypeBuyNow').prop("checked") == true){
		    counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
			}
			tempSearchStr += extraString+' Buy Nows';
			extraString = '';
		}
		if($('#chkSaleTypeCloseout').prop("checked") == true){
		    counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
			}
			tempSearchStr += extraString+' Closeouts';
			extraString = '';
		}
		if($('#chkSaleTypePending').prop("checked") == true){
		    counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
			}
			tempSearchStr += extraString+' Pending';
			extraString = '';
		}
		if($('#chkSaleTypeOffer').prop("checked") == true){
		    counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
			}
			tempSearchStr += extraString+' Offers';
			extraString = '';
		}
		if($('#chkBargainBin').prop("checked") == true){
		    counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
			}
			tempSearchStr += extraString+' Bargain Bins';
			extraString = '';
		}

		if(type == 'inner'){
			return tempSearchStr;
		}
		else{
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				$('#counterVal').html('');
				$('#finalSearchResult').html('');
				$('#counterVal').html(counter1);
				$('#finalSearchResult').html(tempSearchStr);
				//$('#searchResult').html('');
				//$('#searchResult').html("<b id='counterValBTag'><span id='counterVal'>"+counter1+"</span> filters enabled.</b><a href='javascript:void(0)' onClick='showAllFilter()'>Show all filters.</a> <a href='javascript:void(0)' onClick='ToggleSearchPanel()' id='aLinkSearch'>Show search screen</a> <span id='finalSearchResult' style='display:none'>"+tempSearchStr+"</span>");
				/*if(tempSearchStr.length > maxCharacterDisplay){
					$('#searchResult').html("<a data-rel='tooltip' data-placement='bottom' style='color:#393939;text-decoration:none;' href='javascript:void(0)' class='tooltip-info' title='"+tempSearchStr.replace(/(<([^>]+)>)/ig,"")+"'><b><span id='counterVal'>"+counter+"</span> filters enabled</b>: Showing domains with <span id='finalSearchResult' style='display:none;'>"+tempSearchStr+"</span>"+tempSearchStr.substring(0, maxCharacterDisplay)+"...</a>");
				}
				else{
					$('#searchResult').html("<a data-rel='tooltip' data-placement='bottom' style='color:#393939;text-decoration:none;' href='javascript:void(0)' class='tooltip-info'><b><span id='counterVal'>"+counter+"</span> filters enabled</b>: Showing domains with <span id='finalSearchResult' style='display:none'>"+tempSearchStr+"</span>"+tempSearchStr+"</a>");	
				}*/
			}
		}
	}
	else{

		}
	}

function ClearTopicalCategories()
{
	$("#parentTopicalCategory").val('');
	$("#childTopicalCategory").val('');
}

function ChildTopicalCategoryChanged(x)
{
	$("#childTopicalCategory").val(x);
}


function SetParentTopicalCategoryTo(x)
{
	$("#parentTopicalCategory").val(x);
}

function showSearchResultMajesticSeoMetrics(type){
		var seperator = '';
		if(jQuery('#searchResult').html() != ''){
			if(jQuery('#counterVal').html() != ''){
				var counter1 = eval(jQuery('#counterVal').html());
			}

			if(jQuery('#finalSearchResult').html() != ''){
				var seperator = seperatorVal;
				var tempSearchStr = jQuery('#finalSearchResult').html();
			}
		}
		else{
			var seperator = seperatorVal;
			var counter1 = counter;
			var tempSearchStr = '';
		}
		if(type == 'inner'){
			tempSearchStr = '';
		}
		
		
		if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitCitationFlow").val()) != 0 && Math.round($("#upperLimitCitationFlow").val()) != 0){
			counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
			}
			tempSearchStr += 'Citation Flow from '+Math.round($("#lowerLimitCitationFlow").val()) +' to '+ Math.round($("#upperLimitCitationFlow").val());
		}
		else{
			if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitCitationFlow").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'Citation Flow more than '+Math.round($("#lowerLimitCitationFlow").val());
			}
			else if(Math.round($("#upperLimitCitationFlow").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'Citation Flow less than '+ Math.round($("#upperLimitCitationFlow").val());
			}
		}

		if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitTrustFlow").val()) != 0 && Math.round($("#upperLimitTrustFlow").val()) != 0){
			counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
			}
			tempSearchStr += 'Trust Flow from '+Math.round($("#lowerLimitTrustFlow").val()) +' to '+ Math.round($("#upperLimitTrustFlow").val());
		}
		else{
			if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitTrustFlow").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'Trust Flow more than '+Math.round($("#lowerLimitTrustFlow").val());
			}
			else if(Math.round($("#upperLimitTrustFlow").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'Trust Flow less than '+ Math.round($("#upperLimitTrustFlow").val());
			}
		}

		if( $("#lowerLimitTFCFRatio").val() != 0 && $("#upperLimitTFCFRatio").val() != 0){
			counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
			}
			tempSearchStr += 'TF/CF Ratio from '+$("#lowerLimitTFCFRatio").val() +' to '+ $("#upperLimitTFCFRatio").val();
		}
		else{
			if( $("#lowerLimitTFCFRatio").val() != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'TF/CF Ratio more than '+$("#lowerLimitTFCFRatio").val();
			}
			else if(Math.round($("#upperLimitTFCFRatio").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'TF/CF Ratio less than '+ $("#upperLimitTFCFRatio").val();
			}
		}

		if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitMajBackLinks").val()) != 0 && Math.round($("#upperLimitMajBackLinks").val()) != 0){
			counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';

			tempSearchStr += 'Back Links from '+Math.round($("#lowerLimitMajBackLinks").val()) +' to '+ Math.round($("#upperLimitMajBackLinks").val());

<script language="javascript">
function SelectAuctionSources(mode)
{
	if(mode == 'all')
	{
		var checkAllAuctions = true;
	}
	else
	if(mode == 'none')
	{
		var checkAllAuctions = false;
	}
	else
	{
		return;
	}

	$('input[name=chkShowTypeGodaddy]').attr('checked', checkAllAuctions);
	$('input[name=chkShowTypeNameJet]').attr('checked', checkAllAuctions);	
	$('input[name=chkShowTypeSnapNames]').attr('checked', checkAllAuctions);
	$('input[name=chkShowTypeSedo]').attr('checked', checkAllAuctions);
	$('input[name=chkShowTypeDynaDot]').attr('checked', checkAllAuctions);
	$('input[name=chkShowTypeNameSilo]').attr('checked', checkAllAuctions);
	$('input[name=chkShowTypeNamePal]').attr('checked', checkAllAuctions);
	$('input[name=chkShowTypeHuntingMoon]').attr('checked', checkAllAuctions);
	$('input[name=chkShowTypeDomainMarket]').attr('checked', checkAllAuctions);
	$('input[name=chkShowTypeParkIo]').attr('checked', checkAllAuctions);
	$('input[name=chkShowTypeDropCatch]').attr('checked', checkAllAuctions);
	$('input[name=chkShowTypeFlippa]').attr('checked', checkAllAuctions);
}

function showSearchResultDomainSourceAdvanced(type){
	var totalCheckedValDomainSource = 12;
	var checkboxCounterDomainSource = 0;
	
	if($('#chkShowTypeGodaddy').prop("checked") == true){
	    checkboxCounterDomainSource++;
	}
	if($('#chkShowTypeNameJet').prop("checked") == true){
	    checkboxCounterDomainSource++;
	}
	if($('#chkShowTypeSnapNames').prop("checked") == true){
	    checkboxCounterDomainSource++;
	}
	if($('#chkShowTypeSedo').prop("checked") == true){
	    checkboxCounterDomainSource++;
	}
	if($('#chkShowTypeDynaDot').prop("checked") == true){
	    checkboxCounterDomainSource++;
	}
	if($('#chkShowTypeNameSilo').prop("checked") == true){
	    checkboxCounterDomainSource++;
	}
	if($('#chkShowTypeNamePal').prop("checked") == true){
	    checkboxCounterDomainSource++;
	}
	if($('#chkShowTypeHuntingMoon').prop("checked") == true){
	    checkboxCounterDomainSource++;
	}
	if($('#chkShowTypeDomainMarket').prop("checked") == true){
	    checkboxCounterDomainSource++;
	}
	if($('#chkShowTypeParkIo').prop("checked") == true){
	    checkboxCounterDomainSource++;
	}
	if($('#chkShowTypeDropCatch').prop("checked") == true){
	    checkboxCounterDomainSource++;
	}
	if($('#chkShowTypeFlippa').prop("checked") == true){
	    checkboxCounterDomainSource++;
	}

	if(checkboxCounterDomainSource <= totalCheckedValDomainSource-1){
		var seperator = '';
		if(jQuery('#searchResult').html() != ''){
			if(jQuery('#counterVal').html() != ''){
				var counter1 = eval(jQuery('#counterVal').html());
			}

			if(jQuery('#finalSearchResult').html() != ''){
				var seperator = seperatorVal;
				var tempSearchStr = jQuery('#finalSearchResult').html();
			}
		}
		else{
			var seperator = seperatorVal;
			var counter1 = counter;
			var tempSearchStr = '';
		}
		if(type == 'inner'){
			tempSearchStr = '';
		}
		
		var extraString = ' ';

		if($('#chkShowTypeGodaddy').prop("checked") == true){
		    counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
			}
			tempSearchStr += extraString+' GoDaddy';
			extraString = '';
		}
		if($('#chkShowTypeNameJet').prop("checked") == true){
		    counter1++;

				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
			}
			tempSearchStr += extraString+' NameJet';
			extraString = '';
		}
		if($('#chkShowTypeSnapNames').prop("checked") == true){
		    counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
			}
			tempSearchStr += extraString+' SnapNames';
			extraString = '';
		}
		if($('#chkShowTypeSedo').prop("checked") == true){
		    counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
			}
			tempSearchStr += extraString+' Sedo';
			extraString = '';
		}
		if($('#chkShowTypeDynaDot').prop("checked") == true){
		    counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
			}
			tempSearchStr += extraString+' DynaDot';
			extraString = '';
		}
		if($('#chkShowTypeNameSilo').prop("checked") == true){
		    counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
			}
			tempSearchStr += extraString+' Name Silo';
			extraString = '';
		}
		if($('#chkShowTypeNamePal').prop("checked") == true){
		    counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
			}
			tempSearchStr += extraString+' Name Pal';
			extraString = '';
		}
		if($('#chkShowTypeHuntingMoon').prop("checked") == true){
		    counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
			}
			tempSearchStr += extraString+' Hunting Moon';
			extraString = '';
		}
		if($('#chkShowTypeDomainMarket').prop("checked") == true){
		    counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
			}
			tempSearchStr += extraString+' Domain Market';
			extraString = '';
		}
		if($('#chkShowTypeParkIo').prop("checked") == true){

	else{

function showSearchResultMiscellanceAdvance2(type){
	var seperator = '';
	if(jQuery('#searchResult').html() != ''){
		if(jQuery('#counterVal').html() != ''){
			var counter1 = eval(jQuery('#counterVal').html());
		}

		if(jQuery('#finalSearchResult').html() != ''){
			var seperator = seperatorVal;
			var tempSearchStr = jQuery('#finalSearchResult').html();
		}
	}
	else{
		var seperator = seperatorVal;
		var counter1 = counter;
		var tempSearchStr = '';
	}
	if(type == 'inner'){
		tempSearchStr = '';
	}

	var extraString = '';

	if($('#chkHideAdult').prop("checked") == true){
	    counter1++;
		if(tempSearchStr!=''){
			tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
		}
		tempSearchStr += extraString+' Hide Adult';
		extraString = '';
	}
	if($('#chkAllowDashes').prop("checked") == false){
	    counter1++;

		tempSearchStr += extraString+' Disallow domains with dashes';
		extraString = '';
	}
	if($('#chkOnlyDigits').prop("checked") == true){

			tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
		}
		tempSearchStr += extraString+' Hide Spammy Domains';
		extraString = '';
	}
	if($('#chkRequireGoogleIndex').prop("checked") == true){

		extraString = '';

	    counter1++;

		}
		tempSearchStr += extraString+' Hide domains with digits';
		extraString = '';
	}
	if($('#chkHideBrand').prop("checked") == true){
	    counter1++;

			tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';

		tempSearchStr += extraString+' Hide domains with branded keywords';
		extraString = '';
	}
	if($('#chkRequireDomainAvailable').prop("checked") == true){

			tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';

		tempSearchStr += extraString+' Only show Available domains';
		extraString = '';

	if($('#chkRequireGoogleNews').prop("checked") == true){

		extraString = '';
	}

	if($('#chkRequireMajesticMillion').prop("checked") == true){

		extraString = '';

	if(type == 'inner'){

	}
	else{

<script language="javascript">
function showSearchResultAnchorTextBox(type){
	var seperator = '';
	if(jQuery('#searchResult').html() != ''){
		if(jQuery('#counterVal').html() != ''){
			var counter1 = eval(jQuery('#counterVal').html());
		}

		if(jQuery('#finalSearchResult').html() != ''){
			var seperator = seperatorVal;
			var tempSearchStr = jQuery('#finalSearchResult').html();
		}
	}
	else{
		var seperator = seperatorVal;
		var counter1 = counter;
		var tempSearchStr = '';
	}
	if(type == 'inner'){
		tempSearchStr = '';
	}

	if($("#anchorTextKeyword").val() != ''){
		counter1++;
		if(tempSearchStr!=''){
			tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
		}
		tempSearchStr += 'Anchor Text Keyword Entered: <b>'+$('#anchorTextKeyword').val()+'</b>';
	}

	if(type == 'inner'){
		return tempSearchStr;
	}
	else{
		if(tempSearchStr != ''){
			$('#counterVal').html('');
			$('#finalSearchResult').html('');
			$('#counterVal').html(counter1);
			$('#finalSearchResult').html(tempSearchStr);
		}
	}
}

</script>

	<div class="widget-header">

	function showSearchResultSocialMetrics(type){
		
		if(jQuery('#searchResult').html() != ''){
			if(jQuery('#counterVal').html() != ''){
				var counter1 = eval(jQuery('#counterVal').html());
			}

			if(jQuery('#finalSearchResult').html() != ''){
				var seperator = seperatorVal;
				var tempSearchStr = jQuery('#finalSearchResult').html();
			}
		}
		else{
			var seperator = seperatorVal;
			var counter1 = counter;
			var tempSearchStr = '';
		}
		if(type == 'inner'){
			tempSearchStr = '';
		}
		
		if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitSocTotal").val()) != 0 && Math.round($("#upperLimitSocTotal").val()) != 0){
			counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';	
			}
			tempSearchStr += 'Total Shares from '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitSocTotal").val())) +' to '+ number_format(Math.round($("#upperLimitSocTotal").val()));
		}
		else{
			if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitSocTotal").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';	
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'Total Shares more than '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitSocTotal").val()));
			}
			else if(Math.round($("#upperLimitSocTotal").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';	
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'Total Shares less than '+ number_format(Math.round($("#upperLimitSocTotal").val()));
			}
		}

		if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitSocFbTotal").val()) != 0 && Math.round($("#upperLimitSocFbTotal").val()) != 0){
			counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';	
			}
			tempSearchStr += 'Total Facebook Shares from '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitSocFbTotal").val())) +' to '+ number_format(Math.round($("#upperLimitSocFbTotal").val()));
		}
		else{
			if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitSocFbTotal").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';	
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'Total Facebook Shares more than '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitSocFbTotal").val()));
			}
			else if(Math.round($("#upperLimitSocFbTotal").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';	
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'Total Facebook Shares less than '+ number_format(Math.round($("#upperLimitSocFbTotal").val()));
			}
		}


		if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitSocFbShare").val()) != 0 && Math.round($("#upperLimitSocFbShare").val()) != 0){
			counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';	
			}
			tempSearchStr += 'Facebook Shares from '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitSocFbShare").val())) +' to '+ number_format(Math.round($("#upperLimitSocFbShare").val()));
		}
		else{
			if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitSocFbShare").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';	
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'Facebook Shares more than '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitSocFbShare").val()));
			}
			else if(Math.round($("#upperLimitSocFbShare").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';	
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'Facebook Shares less than '+ number_format(Math.round($("#upperLimitSocFbShare").val()));
			}
		}



		if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitSocPinterest").val()) != 0 && Math.round($("#upperLimitSocPinterest").val()) != 0){
			counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';	
			}
			tempSearchStr += 'Total Pins from '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitSocPinterest").val())) +' to '+ number_format(Math.round($("#upperLimitSocPinterest").val()));
		}
		else{
			if( Math.round($("#lowerLimitSocPinterest").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';	
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'Total Pins more than '+number_format(Math.round($("#lowerLimitSocPinterest").val()));
			}
			else if(Math.round($("#upperLimitSocPinterest").val()) != 0){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr != ''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';	
				}
				tempSearchStr += 'Total Pins less than '+ number_format(Math.round($("#upperLimitSocPinterest").val()));
			}
		}


		if(type == 'inner'){
			return tempSearchStr;
		}
		else{
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				$('#counterVal').html('');
				$('#finalSearchResult').html('');
				$('#counterVal').html(counter1);
				$('#finalSearchResult').html(tempSearchStr);
				//$('#searchResult').html('');
				//$('#searchResult').html("<b id='counterValBTag'><span id='counterVal'>"+counter1+"</span> filters enabled.</b> <a href='javascript:void(0)' onClick='showAllFilter()'>Show all filters.</a> <a href='javascript:void(0)' onClick='ToggleSearchPanel()' id='aLinkSearch'>Show search screen</a> <span id='finalSearchResult' style='display:none'>"+tempSearchStr+"</span>");
				/*if(tempSearchStr.length > maxCharacterDisplay){
					$('#searchResult').html("<a data-rel='tooltip' data-placement='bottom' style='color:#393939;text-decoration:none;' href='javascript:void(0)' class='tooltip-info' title='"+tempSearchStr.replace(/(<([^>]+)>)/ig,"")+"'><b><span id='counterVal'>"+counter+"</span> filters enabled</b>: Showing domains with <span id='finalSearchResult' style='display:none;'>"+tempSearchStr+"</span>"+tempSearchStr.substring(0, maxCharacterDisplay)+"...</a>");
				}
				else{
					$('#searchResult').html("<a data-rel='tooltip' data-placement='bottom' style='color:#393939;text-decoration:none;' href='javascript:void(0)' class='tooltip-info'><b><span id='counterVal'>"+counter+"</span> filters enabled</b>: Showing domains with <span id='finalSearchResult' style='display:none'>"+tempSearchStr+"</span>"+tempSearchStr+"</a>");	
				}*/
			}
		}
	}
</script>

<script language="javascript">

    function ClearIndustries() {
        $("#parentCategory").val('');
        $(".childCategory").val('');
    }

    function ChildCategoryChanged(x, id) {
        $("#" + id).val(x);
    }

    function removeChildCategoryTableRows(level) {
        for (var i = 1; i <= 4; i++) {
            $('#childCategoryTr_' + (level + i)).remove();
        }
    }

    function ParentCategoryChanged(x, level, oldValue) {
        //$select = $("#childCategory");
        //$select.empty();
        //$select.append("<option value=''>Choose Sub Industry</option>");


        if (x != '') {
            $.ajax({
                "dataType": 'html',
                "type": "POST",
                "url": "https://www.domcop.com/service/getSubIndustryCategory.php",
                "data": {
                    __csrf_token: 'G5qNoXQfhx3XiE8gXyddt3U6AOwSU51kTx2FcmsJ81dEcYq1OJiF86Sne4td5Nin',
                    val: x,
                    level: level,
                    oldValue: oldValue
                },
                "success": function (data) {
                    removeChildCategoryTableRows(level);
                    $('#IndustryCategory tr:last').after(data);
                }
            });
        } else {
            removeChildCategoryTableRows(level);
        }
    }

    function ParentCategoryChanged1(tempstr) {
        //$select = $("#childCategory");
        //$select.empty();
        //$select.append("<option value=''>Choose Sub Industry</option>");


        $.ajax({
            "dataType": 'html',
            "type": "POST",
            "url": "https://www.domcop.com/service/getSubIndustryCategory.php",
            "data": {
                __csrf_token: 'G5qNoXQfhx3XiE8gXyddt3U6AOwSU51kTx2FcmsJ81dEcYq1OJiF86Sne4td5Nin',
                tempstr: tempstr
            },
            "success": function (data) {
                var level = 1;
                removeChildCategoryTableRows(level);
                $('#IndustryCategory tr:last').after(data);
                ReDrawTable();
                //$select.append(data);
            }
        });
    }

    function showSearchResultIndustry(type) {

        if (jQuery('#searchResult').html() != '') {
            if (jQuery('#counterVal').html() != '') {
                var counter1 = eval(jQuery('#counterVal').html());
            }

            if (jQuery('#finalSearchResult').html() != '') {
                var seperator = seperatorVal;
                var tempSearchStr = jQuery('#finalSearchResult').html();
            }
        } else {
            var seperator = seperatorVal;
            var counter1 = counter;
            var tempSearchStr = '';
        }
        if (type == 'inner') {
            tempSearchStr = '';
            var seperator = ' &nbsp; <b>></b> &nbsp; ';
        }

        if ($("#parentCategory").val() != '') {
            counter1++;
            if (tempSearchStr != '') {
                tempSearchStr += ' ' + seperator + ' ';
            }
            tempSearchStr += $('select#parentCategory option:selected').text();
        }
        if ($('#childCategory_2').length) {
            if ($("#childCategory_2").val() != '') {
                counter1++;
                if (tempSearchStr != '') {
                    tempSearchStr += ' ' + seperator + ' ';
                }
                tempSearchStr += $('select#childCategory_2 option:selected').text();
            }
        }
        if ($('#childCategory_3').length) {
            if ($("#childCategory_3").val() != '') {
                counter1++;
                if (tempSearchStr != '') {
                    tempSearchStr += ' ' + seperator + ' ';
                }
                tempSearchStr += $('select#childCategory_3 option:selected').text();
            }
        }
        if ($('#childCategory_4').length) {
            if ($("#childCategory_4").val() != '') {
                counter1++;
                if (tempSearchStr != '') {
                    tempSearchStr += ' ' + seperator + ' ';
                }
                tempSearchStr += $('select#childCategory_4 option:selected').text();
            }
        }
        if ($('#childCategory_5').length) {
            if ($("#childCategory_5").val() != '') {
                counter1++;
                if (tempSearchStr != '') {
                    tempSearchStr += ' ' + seperator + ' ';
                }
                tempSearchStr += $('select#childCategory_5 option:selected').text();
            }
        }

        if (type == 'inner') {
            return tempSearchStr;
        } else {
            if (tempSearchStr != '') {
                $('#counterVal').html('');
                $('#finalSearchResult').html('');
                $('#counterVal').html(counter1);
                $('#finalSearchResult').html(tempSearchStr);
                //$('#searchResult').html('');
                //$('#searchResult').html("<b id='counterValBTag'><span id='counterVal'>"+counter1+"</span> filters enabled.</b> <a href='javascript:void(0)' onClick='showAllFilter()'>Show all filters.</a> <a href='javascript:void(0)' onClick='ToggleSearchPanel()' id='aLinkSearch'>Show search screen</a> <span id='finalSearchResult' style='display:none'>"+tempSearchStr+"</span>");
                /*if(tempSearchStr.length > maxCharacterDisplay){
                    $('#searchResult').html("<a data-rel='tooltip' data-placement='bottom' style='color:#393939;text-decoration:none;' href='javascript:void(0)' class='tooltip-info' title='"+tempSearchStr.replace(/(<([^>]+)>)/ig,"")+"'><b><span id='counterVal'>"+counter+"</span> filters enabled</b>: Showing domains with <span id='finalSearchResult' style='display:none;'>"+tempSearchStr+"</span>"+tempSearchStr.substring(0, maxCharacterDisplay)+"...</a>");
                }
                else{
                    $('#searchResult').html("<a data-rel='tooltip' data-placement='bottom' style='color:#393939;text-decoration:none;' href='javascript:void(0)' class='tooltip-info'><b><span id='counterVal'>"+counter+"</span> filters enabled</b>: Showing domains with <span id='finalSearchResult' style='display:none'>"+tempSearchStr+"</span>"+tempSearchStr+"</a>");
                }*/
            }
        }
    }
</script>

	<div class="widget-header">
		<h5 class="smaller">Geo Domains</h5>

		<div class="widget-toolbar">
			<small>
			 <a href="#" onclick="javascript: return false;" data-rel="tooltip" data-container="body" class="tooltip-info" data-placement="left" title="" data-original-title="You can find domains that have the names of cities, states, counties, regions or countries in their name. An exact match finds only domains that exactly match a location (e.g. paris.com), while a partial match finds domains that partially match a location (e.g. myparistrip.com). Select a country if you only want to target locations from a specific country">?</a></small>
			| <a href="#" data-action="collapse"><i class="icon-chevron-up" id="sourceCollapsor"></i></a>
		</div>

	<div class="widget-body">
		<div class="widget-main padding-6">
			<table width="100%" border="0">

<script language="javascript">

function showSearchResultGeoDomain(type){
	
	var seperator = seperatorVal;
	if(jQuery('#searchResult').html() != ''){
		if(jQuery('#counterVal').html() != ''){
			var counter1 = eval(jQuery('#counterVal').html());
		}

		if(jQuery('#finalSearchResult').html() != ''){
			var seperator = seperatorVal;
			var tempSearchStr = jQuery('#finalSearchResult').html();
		}
	}
	else{
		var seperator = seperatorVal;
		var counter1 = counter;
		var tempSearchStr = '';
	}
	if(type == 'inner'){
		tempSearchStr = '';
	}
	
	var extraString = '';

	if($('#chkRequireGeoDomain').prop("checked") == true){
	    counter1++;
		if(tempSearchStr != ''){
			tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
		}
		tempSearchStr += extraString+' Show partial match Geo Domains';
		extraString = '';
	}
	if($('#chkRequireMatchGeoDomain').prop("checked") == true){
	    counter1++;
		if(tempSearchStr != ''){
			tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
		}
		tempSearchStr += extraString+' Show exact match Geo Domains';
		extraString = '';
	}
	if ($('#geoName').length){
		if($("#geoName").val() != ''){
			counter1++;
			if(tempSearchStr != ''){
				tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';	
			}
			tempSearchStr += extraString+' Country: '+$('select#geoName option:selected').text();
		}
	}
	
	if(type == 'inner'){
		return tempSearchStr;
	}
	else{
		if(tempSearchStr != ''){
			$('#counterVal').html('');
			$('#finalSearchResult').html('');
			$('#counterVal').html(counter1);
			$('#finalSearchResult').html(tempSearchStr);
		}
	}
}
</script>

	<div class="widget-header">
		<h5 class="smaller">Search</h5>

		<div class="widget-toolbar">
		<small><a href="#" onclick="javascript: ShowKeywordPanel(); return false;" id="KeywordMatchLink" style="text-decoration: none; font-weight: bold;">Keyword</a> | <a href="#" onclick="javascript: ShowPatternPanel(); return false;" id="PatternMatchLink" style="text-decoration: none; font-weight: normal;">Pattern</a></small> <a href="https://www.domcop.com/searchBoxInfo" class="dcPopup cboxElement"><b>?</b></a>
		| <a href="#" data-action="collapse"><i class="icon-chevron-up" id="searchBoxCollapsor"></i></a>
		</div>
	</div>

	<div class="widget-body">
		<div class="widget-main padding-6">
			<input type="hidden" id="searchType" name="searchType">
			<table border="0" width="100%" class="text-right">
			<tbody><tr>
			<td>
				<div id="keywordPanel" style="display:block;">
				<table width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0">
				<tbody><tr>
					<td colspan="2"><textarea name="keyword" id="keyword" class="form-control"></textarea></td>
				</tr>
				<tr>
					<td colspan="2">
						<input type="radio" name="rdKeywordSearchType" id="rdKeywordSearchTypeStarts" value="starts">Starts&nbsp;
						<input type="radio" name="rdKeywordSearchType" id="rdKeywordSearchTypeContains" value="contains" checked="">Contains&nbsp;
						<input type="radio" name="rdKeywordSearchType" id="rdKeywordSearchTypeEnds" value="ends">Ends&nbsp;

				<div id="patternPanel" style="display:none;">
				 
				<br>

function ShowKeywordPanel()
{
	document.getElementById('keywordPanel').style.display = 'block'; 
	document.getElementById('patternPanel').style.display = 'none';
	document.getElementById('KeywordMatchLink').style.fontWeight = 'bold';
	document.getElementById('PatternMatchLink').style.fontWeight = 'normal';	
	document.getElementById('searchType').value = 'keyword';	
}
function ShowPatternPanel()
{
	document.getElementById('keywordPanel').style.display = 'none'; 
	document.getElementById('patternPanel').style.display = 'block';
	document.getElementById('KeywordMatchLink').style.fontWeight = 'normal';
	document.getElementById('PatternMatchLink').style.fontWeight = 'bold';

}
function showSearchResultSearchBox(type){
	var seperator = '';
	if(jQuery('#searchResult').html() != ''){
		if(jQuery('#counterVal').html() != ''){
			var counter1 = eval(jQuery('#counterVal').html());
		}

		if(jQuery('#finalSearchResult').html() != ''){
			var seperator = seperatorVal;
			var tempSearchStr = jQuery('#finalSearchResult').html();
		}
	}
	else{
		var seperator = seperatorVal;
		var counter1 = counter;
		var tempSearchStr = '';
	}
	if(type == 'inner'){
		tempSearchStr = '';
	}

	if($("#keyword").val() != ''){
		counter1++;
		if(tempSearchStr!=''){
			tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
		}
		tempSearchStr += 'Keyword Entered: <b>'+$('#keyword').val()+'</b>';
	}

	if(type == 'inner'){
		return tempSearchStr;
	}
	else{
		if(tempSearchStr != ''){
			$('#counterVal').html('');
			$('#finalSearchResult').html('');
			$('#counterVal').html(counter1);
			$('#finalSearchResult').html(tempSearchStr);
			//$('#searchResult').html('');
			//$('#searchResult').html("<b id='counterValBTag'><span id='counterVal'>"+counter1+"</span> filters enabled.</b> <a href='javascript:void(0)' onClick='showAllFilter()'>Show all filters.</a> <a href='javascript:void(0)' onClick='ToggleSearchPanel()' id='aLinkSearch'>Show search screen</a> <span id='finalSearchResult' style='display:none'>"+tempSearchStr+"</span>");
			/*if(tempSearchStr.length > maxCharacterDisplay){
				$('#searchResult').html("<a data-rel='tooltip' data-placement='bottom' style='color:#393939;text-decoration:none;' href='javascript:void(0)' class='tooltip-info' title='"+tempSearchStr.replace(/(<([^>]+)>)/ig,"")+"'><b><span id='counterVal'>"+counter+"</span> filters enabled</b>: Showing domains with <span id='finalSearchResult' style='display:none;'>"+tempSearchStr+"</span>"+tempSearchStr.substring(0, maxCharacterDisplay)+"...</a>");
			}
			else{
				$('#searchResult').html("<a data-rel='tooltip' data-placement='bottom' style='color:#393939;text-decoration:none;' href='javascript:void(0)' class='tooltip-info'><b><span id='counterVal'>"+counter+"</span> filters enabled</b>: Showing domains with <span id='finalSearchResult' style='display:none'>"+tempSearchStr+"</span>"+tempSearchStr+"</a>");	
			}*/
		}
	}
}

<script language="javascript">
$(document).on('click.ace.widget', '[data-action]', function (ev) {

ev.preventDefault();

var $this = $(this);
var $action = $this.data('action');
var $box = $this.closest('.widget-box');
var event_name = $box.hasClass('collapsed') ? 'show' : 'hide';

//alert(ev.target.id + ' ' + event_name);
if($action == 'collapse')
{
$.ajaxSetup ({cache: false});
$.ajax({type: "GET", url: "https://www.domcop.com/service/setWidgetState.php?id=" + ev.target.id + "&action=" + event_name + "&rand=" + Math.random(), success:function(result){ } });	
}


});
</script>

<script language="javascript">

function ToggleSearchPanel()
{
	if($('#counterVal').html() != '0'){
		if($( "#container-fluid" ).css( "display" ) == 'none'){
			$('.widget-body').show();
			$('#searchResult').hide();
			$('#container-fluid').show();
			$( "#searchPanelIcon" ).addClass("icon-chevron-down").removeClass( "icon-chevron-up" );
			$( "#toggleFilterBtn" ).html('Hide Filter');
		}
		else{
			if(1 != 1){
				$('.widget-body').hide();
			}
			$('#searchResult').show();
			$('#container-fluid').hide();
			$( "#searchPanelIcon" ).removeClass("icon-chevron-down").addClass( "icon-chevron-up" );
			$( "#toggleFilterBtn" ).html('Show Filter');
		}
	}
	else{
		$('#searchResult').hide();
		if($( "#searchPanel" ).hasClass( "collapsed" ))
		{
			ShowSearchPanel();
		}
		else
		{
			HideSearchPanel();
		}
	}
}

function saveNote(id, type,domain){
	var newNoteVal = $('#textarea'+id).val();
	if(newNoteVal == ''){
		alert("Please enter some notes here.");
		$('#textarea'+id).focus();
		return false;
	}
	else{
		$.ajax( {
	                "dataType": 'html',
	                "type": "POST",
				"url": "https://www.domcop.com/service/saveNotes.php",
				"data": {
					__csrf_token: 'G5qNoXQfhx3XiE8gXyddt3U6AOwSU51kTx2FcmsJ81dEcYq1OJiF86Sne4td5Nin',
					newNoteVal:newNoteVal,
					type:type,
					domain:domain
				},
	                "success": function(data) {
	                	var temp = newNoteVal.substring(0, 100);
	                    $("#anotes"+id).tooltip('hide').attr("data-original-title", temp).tooltip('fixTitle').tooltip('show');
	                    $('#iNotes'+id).css('color', 'orange');
						$.colorbox.close();
	                }
	            });
			
	}
}

function HideSearchPanel()
{
	$('#searchResult').hide();
	if($('#counterVal').html() != '0' || $('#counterVal').html() != ''){
		$('#searchResult').show();
	}
	$('#container-fluid').hide();
	$('.widget-body').hide();
	$( "#searchPanel" ).addClass( "collapsed" );
	$( "#searchPanelIcon" ).removeClass("icon-chevron-up").addClass( "icon-chevron-down" );
	$('html, body').animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, 0);
	$( "#toggleFilterBtn" ).html('Show Filter');
	createJsCookie('searchBoxStatus', 'hidden', 365);
}

function ShowSearchPanel()
{
	$('#container-fluid').show();
	$('.widget-body').show();
	$( "#searchPanel" ).removeClass( "collapsed" );
	$( "#searchPanelIcon" ).removeClass("icon-chevron-down").addClass( "icon-chevron-up" );
	$( "#toggleFilterBtn" ).html('Hide Filter');
	createJsCookie('searchBoxStatus', 'shown', 365);
}

function createJsCookie(name, value, days)
{
    var expires;

    if (days) {
        var date = new Date();
        date.setTime(date.getTime() + (days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
        expires = "; expires=" + date.toGMTString();
    } else {
        expires = "";
    }
    document.cookie = escape(name) + "=" + escape(value) + expires + "; path=/";
}

setTimeout('$("#jsMessage").hide("slow");', 10000);

<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">

function number_format (number, decimals, dec_point, thousands_sep) {
    // Strip all characters but numerical ones.
    number = (number + '').replace(/[^0-9+\-Ee.]/g, '');
    var n = !isFinite(+number) ? 0 : +number,
        prec = !isFinite(+decimals) ? 0 : Math.abs(decimals),
        sep = (typeof thousands_sep === 'undefined') ? ',' : thousands_sep,
        dec = (typeof dec_point === 'undefined') ? '.' : dec_point,
        s = '',
        toFixedFix = function (n, prec) {
            var k = Math.pow(10, prec);
            return '' + Math.round(n * k) / k;
        };
    // Fix for IE parseFloat(0.55).toFixed(0) = 0;
    s = (prec ? toFixedFix(n, prec) : '' + Math.round(n)).split('.');

	if (s[0].length > 3) {
        s[0] = s[0].replace(/\B(?=(?:\d{3})+(?!\d))/g, sep);
    }

    if ((s[1] || '').length < prec) {
        s[1] = s[1] || '';
        s[1] += new Array(prec - s[1].length + 1).join('0');
    }
    return s.join(dec);
}

function copyToClipboard(element) {

		//document.getSelection().removeAllRanges();
	if (document.selection) { //IE
		var range = document.body.createTextRange();
		range.moveToElementText(element);
		range.select();
	} else if (window.getSelection) { //others
		var range = document.createRange();
		range.selectNode(element);
		window.getSelection().removeAllRanges();
		window.getSelection().addRange(range);
	}

	setTimeout(function (){
		document.execCommand('copy');
	    document.getSelection().removeAllRanges();
	},0);

}

function createCopyBuffer() {
	let temporaryElement = $('<textarea/>',{
      id: "clipboardBuffer", //options.event.target
    });
	return temporaryElement;
}

function destroyCopyBuffer() {
	$("#clipboardBuffer").remove();
}

function setupCopyEvents() {
// Firefox 1.0+
	var isFirefox = typeof InstallTrigger !== 'undefined';

	$('.copy-clipboard-single').click(function (e) {
		e.preventDefault();
		let elem = $(this).siblings('.big-domain').children('a')[0];
		let text = elem.innerText;
		if(isFirefox){
			let copyBuffer = createCopyBuffer();
			copyBuffer.text(text);
			copyBuffer.appendTo('body');
			copyBuffer.select();
			document.execCommand('copy');
			setTimeout(() => destroyCopyBuffer(), 0);
		} else{
			copyToClipboard(elem);
		}
	});
}

}

//Check if allowed no-recaptcha window is valid

var execSearchWRecaptcha = function (){
	grecaptcha.ready(function (){
			grecaptcha.execute();
			var grecaptchaResponse = null;
			let checkResponseAttempts = 0;
			let checkResponseInterval = setInterval(function (){

				grecaptchaResponse = grecaptcha.getResponse();

				if(grecaptchaResponse.length > 0){
					loadResults(grecaptchaResponse);
					grecaptcha.reset();
					clearInterval(checkResponseInterval);
				}

				if(checkResponseAttempts > 50){
					clearInterval(checkResponseInterval);
				}

			}, 100);
	});
}



	//Controlled Recaptcha

    
		var weNeedRecaptcha = 1 ;
		

	if(!!weNeedRecaptcha){
	$.ajax({
		method: "GET",
		data: "",
		url: "https://www.domcop.com/" + "service/recaptchaRevalidationCheck.php",
		success: function (data){
		var resp = JSON.parse(data);
			if(resp.proveNotRobot){
			    execSearchWRecaptcha();
	} else {
		loadResults(null);
	}
	},
	error: function (error){
		window.lastErr = error;
		console.log("check lastError")
	}
});
	}  else loadResults(null);
	//End Of Check Section





		},

			saveDomainForClipboard(nRow);
		        return nRow;

			    var values = tData[0].split(',');
			    var maxValue = tData[1];
			    //console.log('MaxVal: ' + maxValue);
			    var bars = values.map( function(v) {
			    	  var data = v.split('|');
				  var normalizedV = parseInt((data[0] * 100)/maxValue);
				  //console.log(v + '->' + normalizedV + ' / ' + maxValue);
			      return $('<div>', {
				class: 'sparkline-bar',
				style: "height:" + normalizedV + "%",
				title: "Moz Domain Authority: " + data[0] + " for " + data[1]
			      }).tooltip();
			    });

			    $e.html ( $("<div>", {
			      class: "sparkline-container",
			      html: bars
			    }) );

	jQuery.fn.dataTableExt.oApi.fnSortNeutral = function ( oSettings )
	{
	    /* Remove any current sorting */
	    oSettings.aaSorting = [];

	    /* Sort display arrays so we get them in numerical order */
	    oSettings.aiDisplay.sort( function (x,y) {
		return x-y;
	    } );
	    oSettings.aiDisplayMaster.sort( function (x,y) {
		return x-y;
	    } );

	    /* Redraw */
	    oSettings.oApi._fnReDraw( oSettings );
	};

	jQuery.fn.dataTableExt.oApi.fnProcessingIndicator = function ( oSettings, onoff )
	{
	    if ( typeof( onoff ) == 'undefined' ) {
		onoff = true;
	    }
	    this.oApi._fnProcessingDisplay( oSettings, onoff );
	};

function showAllGroup(buttonId, SelectId, val){
	if(val == 1){
		var rowIdString = '';

		$("#domcop-table .dcTableCheckBox").each(function()
		{
			if(this.checked)
			{
				var parts = this.id.split('|');
				if(parts[0] != null)
				{
					var domain = parts[0].trim();
					if(domain != '')
					{
						rowIdString = rowIdString + domain + ', ';
					}
				}
			}
		});

		if(rowIdString == ''){
			alert("Please select the domains you want to add to the group.");
			return false;
		}
		else{
			$('#'+SelectId).show();
			$('#'+buttonId).attr("style", "display: none !important");
		}
	}
	else{
		$('#'+SelectId).show();
		$('#'+buttonId).attr("style", "display: none !important");
	}
}

function fnAddDomainGroup(){
	var selectGroupVal = $('#DomainGroupSelect').val();
	if(selectGroupVal == 'none'){
		alert("Please select one group.");
		$('#DomainGroupSelect').focus();
		return false;
	}
	else if(selectGroupVal == 'manage'){
		window.location.href = 'https://www.domcop.com/manageGroups?datatype=watchlist';
		return false;
	}
	else{
		var rowIdString = '';

		$("#domcop-table .dcTableCheckBox").each(function()
		{
			if(this.checked)
			{
				var parts = this.id.split('|');
				if(parts[0] != null)
				{
					var domain = parts[0].trim();
					if(domain != '')
					{
						rowIdString = rowIdString + domain + ', ';
					}
				}
			}
		});

		if(rowIdString == ''){
			alert("Please select the domains you want to add to the group.");
			return false;
		}
		else{
			if(confirm('This will add the selected domains to the selected group. Confirm?')){
				$.ajaxSetup ({cache: false});
					$.ajax(
							{
								type: "POST",
								url: "https://www.domcop.com/service/bulkAddGroup.php?mode=add&dataSource=live&rand=" + Math.random(),
								data: {
									__csrf_token: 'G5qNoXQfhx3XiE8gXyddt3U6AOwSU51kTx2FcmsJ81dEcYq1OJiF86Sne4td5Nin',
									searches: rowIdString,
									selectGroupVal: selectGroupVal
								},
								success: function (result) {
									if (String(result).trim() == 'added') {
										$('#jsMessageText').text('The Selected domains have been added to selected group.');
										$('#jsMessage').show(0).delay(10000).hide(0);
									}
					showAllGroup('DomainGroupSelect', 'AddGroupButton', '');
					$('#DomainGroupSelect').val('none');
								}
							}
					);
			}
		}
	}
}

function fnRemoveDomainGroup(){
	if(confirm('This will add the selected domains to the selected group. Confirm?')){

		var rowIdString = '';

		$("#domcop-table .dcTableCheckBox").each(function()
		{
			if(this.checked)
			{
				var parts = this.id.split('|');
				if(parts[0] != null)
				{
					var domain = parts[0].trim();
					if(domain != '')
					{
						rowIdString = rowIdString + domain + ', ';
					}
				}
			}
		});

		$.ajaxSetup ({cache: false});
			$.ajax({
						type: "POST",
						url: "https://www.domcop.com/service/bulkAddGroup.php?mode=remove&dataSource=live&rand=" + Math.random(),
						data: {
							__csrf_token: 'G5qNoXQfhx3XiE8gXyddt3U6AOwSU51kTx2FcmsJ81dEcYq1OJiF86Sne4td5Nin',
							searches: rowIdString
						},
						success: function (result) {
							if (String(result).trim() == 'deleted') {
								$('#jsMessageText').text('The Selected domains have been deleted to selected group.');
								$('#jsMessage').show(0).delay(10000).hide(0);
							}
						}
					}
			);
	}
}

function fnRecheckAvailability(){
	var rowIdString = '';

	$("#domcop-table .dcTableCheckBox").each(function()
	{
		if(this.checked)
		{
			var parts = this.id.split('|');
			if(parts[0] != null)
			{
				var domain = parts[0].trim();
				if(domain != '')
				{
					rowIdString = rowIdString + domain + ', ';
				}
			}
		}
	});

	$.ajaxSetup ({cache: false});
		$.ajax({
			type: "POST",
			url: "https://www.domcop.com/service/crawlDomainRecheckAvailability.php?dataSource=live&mode=updated&rand=" + Math.random(),
			data: {
				__csrf_token: 'G5qNoXQfhx3XiE8gXyddt3U6AOwSU51kTx2FcmsJ81dEcYq1OJiF86Sne4td5Nin',
				domains: rowIdString
			},
			success: function (result) {
		if(String(result).trim() == 'updated'){
			var oTable = $('#domcop-table').dataTable();
			oTable.fnDraw();
			$('#jsMessageText').text('The Selected domains have been setup to recheck whether they are still available.');
			$('#jsMessage').show(0).delay( 10000 ).hide(0);
		}
			}
		});
}

function handleServerError( xhr, textStatus, error )
{

    //show error in popup
    console.log('Service Error:' + textStatus);
    if(textStatus == 'parsererror')
    {
        $.colorbox({width:"50%", opacity:"0.1", html:"<div style='padding: 20px;'><div class='alert alert-danger'><i class='icon-exclamation'></i> &nbsp; Something went wrong :(</div><p class='better'>Please do a hard refresh (Chrome: CTRL + F5 - Firefox: SHFT + CTRL + R) on this page. <br/><br/>If you continue seeing this issue, email us at support@domcop.com about this error, mentioning your OS and Browser. <br/><br/></p></div>"});
    }
    else
    if(textStatus == 'timeout')
    {
        $.colorbox({width:"50%", opacity:"0.1", html:"<div style='padding: 20px;'><div class='alert alert-danger'><i class='icon-exclamation'></i> &nbsp; The search is taking a long time to execute</div><p class='better'>Please sit back and relax.<br/> This page will automatically refresh in 5 minutes with the domains found.</p><p>If you continue seeing this popup after the refresh, please check our <a href='https://www.domcop.com/faq/slow-searches'>FAQs on how to speed up the searches</a></p></div>"});
        var oTable = $('#domcop-table').dataTable();
        oTable.fnProcessingIndicator( false );
        setTimeout(function(){ReDrawTable()}, 300000); //5 min = 300000;
    }
    else
    if(xhr.responseText  == 'recaptcha'){
        $.colorbox({width:"50%", opacity:"0.1", html:"<div style='padding: 20px;'><div class='alert alert-danger'><i class='icon-exclamation'></i> &nbsp; Something went wrong :(</div><p class='better'>We were unable to verify recaptcha for this request. <br/> <a href='#' onClick='location.reload();return false;'> Please click here to try again </a></p></div>"});
    }
}

function ShowMessageForRunningQuery()
{
    //show error in popup
    console.log('already running');
    $.colorbox({width:"50%", opacity:"0.1", html:"<div style='padding: 20px;'><div class='alert alert-success'><i class='icon-spinner icon-spin green'></i> &nbsp; The search is running in the background</div><p class='better'>As soon as it is done, the page will automatically refresh with the domains found.</p><p>If you continue seeing this popup for a very long time, please check our <a href='https://www.domcop.com/faq/slow-searches'>FAQs on how to speed up the searches</a></p></div>"});

    var oTable = $('#domcop-table').dataTable();
    oTable.fnProcessingIndicator( false );

    setTimeout(function(){ReDrawTable()}, 10000); //refresh every 10 seconds
}

function AskUserToRefreshPage()
{
    console.log('refresh page');
    setTimeout('location.reload();', 2000); //refresh after 30 seconds
}

function saveDomainForClipboard(row)
{
	var rowIdParts = row.id.split('|');
	if(rowIdParts[2] != '' && rowIdParts[2] != undefined)
	{
		var data = $('#all-domains').html()  + rowIdParts[2] + "\r\n";
		$('#all-domains').html(data);
	}
}

function CheckBoxStateChanged(element)
{
	var anyCheckboxesChecked = false;
	var listOfDomains = '';
	var listOfDomainsSelected = '';
	$("#domcop-table .dcTableCheckBox").each(function()
	{
		var parts = this.id.split('|');
		if(parts[1] != null)
		{
			var domain = parts[1].trim();
			if(domain != '')
			{
				if(this.checked)
				{
					anyCheckboxesChecked = true;
					listOfDomainsSelected = listOfDomainsSelected + "\r\n" + domain;
				}
				listOfDomains = listOfDomains + "\r\n" + domain;
			}

		}
	});
	if(anyCheckboxesChecked)
	{
		if(listOfDomainsSelected.trim() != '')
		{
			$('#all-domains').html(listOfDomainsSelected.trim());
		}
	}
	else
	{
		if(listOfDomains.trim() != '')
		{
			$('#all-domains').html(listOfDomains);
		}
	}
}
