	document.location = "https://www.domcop.com/pricing";
	
}

function AddRecordsToDeleteCrawl()
{
	
		
	if(confirm('This will delete the selected domains from your crawler. Confirm?'))
	{
		//var nNodes = oTable.fnGetNodes( );
		var rowIdString = '';

		$("#domcop-table .dcTableCheckBox").each(function()
		{
			if(this.checked)
			{
				var parts = this.id.split('|');
				if(parts[0] != null)
				{
					var domainId = parts[0].trim();
					if(domainId != '')
					{
						rowIdString = rowIdString + domainId + ', ';
					}
				}
			}
		});
		$.ajaxSetup ({cache: false});
		$.ajax({
			type: "POST",
			url: "https://www.domcop.com/service/bulkCrawlDelete.php?dataSource=live&mode=delete&rand=" + Math.random(),
				data: {
					__csrf_token: 'G5qNoXQfhx3XiE8gXyddt3U6AOwSU51kTx2FcmsJ81dEcYq1OJiF86Sne4td5Nin',
					domains: rowIdString
				},
			success:function(result){
					if (String(result).trim() == 'deleted') {
					$('#jsMessageText').text('Selected domains were successfully Deleted.');
					$('#jsMessage').show(0).delay( 10000 ).hide(0);
					$(".dcTableCheckBox").attr('checked', false);
				}
			}
			});
		ReDrawTable();

	}
	
		
}

function AddRecordsToWatchlist()
{
	
		
	if(confirm('This will add the selected domains to your watchlist. Confirm?'))
	{
		//var nNodes = oTable.fnGetNodes( );
		var rowIdString = '';

		$("#domcop-table .dcTableCheckBox").each(function()
		{
			if(this.checked)
			{
				var parts = this.id.split('|');
				if(parts[1] != null)
				{
					var domain = parts[1].trim();
					if(domain != '')
					{
						rowIdString = rowIdString + domain + ', ';
						var watchlistIcon = document.getElementById("fav-" + domain);
						$(watchlistIcon).removeClass("icon-star-empty").addClass("icon-star");
					}
				}
			}
		});
		$.ajaxSetup ({cache: false});
			$.ajax({
				type: "POST",
				url: "https://www.domcop.com/service/bulkFavorites.php?dataSource=live&mode=add&rand=" + Math.random(),
				data: {
					__csrf_token: 'G5qNoXQfhx3XiE8gXyddt3U6AOwSU51kTx2FcmsJ81dEcYq1OJiF86Sne4td5Nin',
					domains: rowIdString
				},
				success: function (result) {
					if (String(result).trim() == 'added') {
						$('#jsMessageText').text('Selected domains were successfully added to your watchlist.');
						$('#jsMessage').show(0).delay(10000).hide(0);
					}
				}
			});

	}
	
		
}

function RemoveRecordsFromWatchlist()
{
	if(confirm('This will remove the selected domains from your watchlist. Confirm?'))
	{
		var rowIdString = '';
		$("#domcop-table .dcTableCheckBox").each(function()
		{
			if(this.checked)
			{
				var parts = this.id.split('|');
				if(parts[0] != null)
				{
					var domain = parts[1].trim();
					var domainId = parts[0].trim();
					if(domain != '')
					{
						rowIdString = rowIdString + 'id[]=' + domainId + '&';
						var watchlistIcon = document.getElementById("fav-" + domain);
						$(watchlistIcon).removeClass("icon-star").addClass("icon-star-empty");
					}
				}
			}
		});
		if(rowIdString != '')
		{
			$.ajaxSetup ({cache: false});
			var url = "https://www.domcop.com/service/deleteFavorites.php?" + rowIdString;

			$.ajax({url: url, success:function(result)
			{
				if(String(result).trim() == 'deleted')
				{

					//refresh;
					var oTable = $('#domcop-table').dataTable();
					oTable.fnDraw();
					$(".dcTableCheckBox").attr('checked', false);
					$('#jsMessageText').text('Selected domains were successfully removed from your watchlist.');
					$('#jsMessage').show(0).delay( 10000 ).hide(0);

				}
			}});
		}
	}
}

function RemoveRecordsFromMyDomains(){
	if(confirm('This will remove the selected domains from your list. Confirm?'))
	{
		var rowIdString = '';
		$("#domcop-table .dcTableCheckBox").each(function()
		{
			if(this.checked)
			{
				var parts = this.id.split('|');
				if(parts[0] != null)
				{
					var domain = parts[1].trim();
					var domainId = parts[0].trim();
					if(domain != '')
					{
						rowIdString = rowIdString + 'id[]=' + domainId + '&';
					}
				}
			}
		});
		if(rowIdString != '')
		{
			$.ajaxSetup ({cache: false});
			var url = "https://www.domcop.com/service/deleteMyDomains.php?" + rowIdString;

			$.ajax({url: url, success:function(result)
			{
				if(String(result).trim() == 'deleted')
				{
					//refresh;
					var oTable = $('#domcop-table').dataTable();
					oTable.fnDraw();
					$(".dcTableCheckBox").attr('checked', false);
					$('#jsMessageText').text('Selected domains were successfully removed from your list.');
					$('#jsMessage').show(0).delay( 10000 ).hide(0);

				}
			}});
		}
	}
}

function RemoveAllRecordsFromMyDomains(){

	{
		$.ajaxSetup ({cache: false});
		var url = "https://www.domcop.com/service/deleteMyDomains.php?id[]=deleteAll";

		$.ajax({url: url, success:function(result)
		{

			{
				//refresh;
				var oTable = $('#domcop-table').dataTable();
				oTable.fnDraw();
				$(".dcTableCheckBox").attr('checked', false);
				$('#jsMessageText').text('All domains were successfully removed from your list.');
				$('#jsMessage').show(0).delay( 10000 ).hide(0);

			}
		}});
	}
}

function SaveSearchCookie()
{
	var x = GetSearchParams();
	x = x.replace(/params\[/g, "");
	x =  x.replace(/\]/g, "");
	createCookie("SrchPrmsCk",x,365);
}

function ReDrawTable()
{
	
	//get params - compress and store it in cookie
	var x = GetSearchParams();
	x = x.replace(/params\[/g, "");
	x =  x.replace(/\]/g, "");

	createCookie("SrchPrmsCk",x,365);

	
		
		jQuery('#counterVal').html('0');
		jQuery('#finalSearchResult').html('');
		showSearchResultDomain('1','');
		showSearchResultMozMetrics('');
		showSearchResultMajesticSeoMetrics('');
		showSearchResultSocialMetrics('');
		
					
		showSearchResultAnchorTextBox('');
		showSearchResultAlexaMetrics('');
		showSearchResultSemRushMetrics('');
		showSearchResultExtensions('');
		
				
			showSearchResultAuctionTypes('');
			showSearchResultDomainSourceAdvanced('');
		
				
		showSearchResultMiscellanceAdvance2('');
		//showSearchResultMiscellanceAdvance1('');
		showSearchResultIndustry('');
		showSearchResultSlider('');
		
						
			//showSearchResultLanguageSource('');
                        showSearchResultWebsiteLanguage('');
                        showSearchResultBacklinksLanguage('');
			showSearchResultGeoDomain('');
			showSearchResultSearchBox('');
		
			if(!1){
				
				$('.widget-body').hide();
				
			}
		
		if(jQuery('#counterVal').html() != '0'){
			$('#resetButtonHeader').removeClass('btn-primary');
			$('#resetButtonHeader').addClass('btn-danger');
			$('.widget-body').show();
			$('#container-fluid').hide();
			$('#searchResult').show();
			$( "#searchPanel" ).removeClass( "collapsed" );
			$( "#searchPanelIcon" ).removeClass("icon-chevron-down").addClass( "icon-chevron-up" );
			$( "#toggleFilterBtn" ).html('Show Filter');
			createJsCookie('searchBoxStatus', 'shown', 365);
		}
		else{
			$('.widget-body').hide();
			$('#searchResult').hide();
			$('#container-fluid').hide();
			$( "#searchPanel" ).addClass( "collapsed" );
			$( "#searchPanelIcon" ).addClass("icon-chevron-down").addClass( "icon-chevron-up" );
			$( "#toggleFilterBtn" ).html('Show Filter');
			createJsCookie('searchBoxStatus', 'shown', 365);
		}
	
		

	var oTable = $('#domcop-table').dataTable();
	oTable.fnDraw();
	
		

}

function fnShowString(){
	jQuery('#finalSearchResult').show();
	jQuery('#counterVal').hide();
	jQuery('#aLinkSearch').hide();
	jQuery('#counterValBTag').hide();
}

function showSearchResultSlider(type){
// console.log("DataSource live")
	var seperator = '';
	if(jQuery('#counterVal').html() != '0'){
		if(jQuery('#counterVal').html() != '0'){
			var counter1 = eval(jQuery('#counterVal').html());
		}

		if(jQuery('#finalSearchResult').html() != ''){
			var seperator = seperatorVal;
			var tempSearchStr = jQuery('#finalSearchResult').html();
		}
	}
	else{
		var seperator = seperatorVal;
		var counter1 = counter;
		var tempSearchStr = '';
	}
	if(type == 'inner'){
		tempSearchStr = '';
	}
	
													

			if($('#sliderEndsIn').slider("values", 0) != 0 || $('#sliderEndsIn').slider("values", 1) !== 14){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr!=''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
				}
				tempSearchStr += ' Ends Date from '+$('#lowerLimitEndsIn').html();

				if($('#sliderEndsIn').slider("values", 1) != 0){
					tempSearchStr += ' to  '+$('#upperLimitEndsIn').html()+' away';
				}
			}
			if($('#sliderEndedInDomain').slider("values", 0) != 0 || $('#sliderEndedInDomain').slider("values", 1) !== 17){
				counter1++;
				if(tempSearchStr!=''){
					tempSearchStr += ' '+seperator+' ';
				}
				tempSearchStr += ' Domain Added from '+$('#lowerLimitEndedInDomain').html();

				if($('#sliderEndedInDomain').slider("values", 1) != 0){
					tempSearchStr += ' to  '+$('#upperLimitEndedInDomain').html()+' away';
				}
			}
		
					

	if(type == 'inner'){
		return tempSearchStr;
	}
	else{
		if(tempSearchStr != ''){
			$('#counterVal').html('');
			$('#finalSearchResult').html('');
			$('#counterVal').html(counter1);
			$('#finalSearchResult').html(tempSearchStr);
			//$('#searchResult').html("<b id='counterValBTag'><span id='counterVal'>"+counter1+"</span> filters enabled.</b> <a href='javascript:void(0)' onClick='ToggleSearchPanel()' id='aLinkSearch'>Show search screen</a> <span id='finalSearchResult' style='display:none'>"+tempSearchStr+"</span>");
			/*if(tempSearchStr.length > maxCharacterDisplay){
				$('#searchResult').html("<a data-rel='tooltip' data-placement='bottom' style='color:#393939;text-decoration:none;' href='javascript:void(0)' class='tooltip-info' title='"+tempSearchStr.replace(/(<([^>]+)>)/ig,"")+"'><b><span id='counterVal'>"+counter+"</span> filters enabled</b>: Showing domains with <span id='finalSearchResult' style='display:none;'>"+tempSearchStr+"</span>"+tempSearchStr.substring(0, maxCharacterDisplay)+"...</a>");
			}
			else{
				$('#searchResult').html("<a data-rel='tooltip' data-placement='bottom' style='color:#393939;text-decoration:none;' href='javascript:void(0)' class='tooltip-info'><b><span id='counterVal'>"+counter+"</span> filters enabled</b>: Showing domains with <span id='finalSearchResult' style='display:none'>"+tempSearchStr+"</span>"+tempSearchStr+"</a>");
			}*/
		}
	}
}

function SaveSearchParams()
{
	var x = GetSearchParams();
	x = x.replace(/params\[/g, "");
	x =  x.replace(/\]/g, "");
	createCookie("SrchPrmsCk",x,365);
}

function createCookie(name,value,days) {
	$.ajaxSetup ({cache: false});
		$.ajax({
			type: "POST",
			url: "https://www.domcop.com/service/create.php?cookie=" + name,
			data: {
				__csrf_token: 'G5qNoXQfhx3XiE8gXyddt3U6AOwSU51kTx2FcmsJ81dEcYq1OJiF86Sne4td5Nin',
				val: value
			},
			success: function (result) {
			}
		});
	}

function eraseCookie(name) {
	$.ajaxSetup ({cache: false});
	$.ajax({url:"https://www.domcop.com/service/clear.php?cookie=" + name, success:function(result){ }});
}

function EeraseCookieThenReset(fn) {
	$.ajaxSetup ({cache: false});
	$.ajax({url:"https://www.domcop.com/service/clear.php?cookie=SrchPrmsCk", success:function(result){ 
		ResetFilters()
	}});
}

function hidePanel()
{
		jQuery("#panel1").hide(500);
		jQuery("#panel2").show(500);
}

function showPanel()
{
		jQuery("#panel1").show(500);
		jQuery("#panel2").hide(500);
}

function SaveSorting()
{
	var oTable = $('#domcop-table').dataTable();
	var sortParam = oTable.fnSettings().aaSorting;
	if(sortParam != '')
	{
		$.ajaxSetup ({cache: false});
		$.ajax({url: "https://www.domcop.com/service/create.php?cookie=sort&data=" + sortParam, success:function(result){ }});
	}

}

function GetSearchParams()
{
	var params = '';

	
        
		

		if(Math.round($("#upperLimitPageRank").val()) < 10 && Math.round($("#upperLimitPageRank").val()) >= 0)
		{
			if($("#upperLimitPageRank").val() != '')
				params += '&params[upperLimitPageRank]=' + Math.round($("#upperLimitPageRank").val());
		}
		if(Math.round($("#lowerLimitPageRank").val()) > 0)
		{
			params += '&params[lowerLimitPageRank]=' + Math.round($("#lowerLimitPageRank").val());
		}



		if(Math.round($("#upperLimitDomainAuthority").val()) < 100 && Math.round($("#upperLimitDomainAuthority").val()) >= 0)
		{
			if($("#upperLimitDomainAuthority").val() != '')
				params += '&params[upperLimitDomainAuthority]=' + Math.round($("#upperLimitDomainAuthority").val());
		}
		if(Math.round($("#lowerLimitDomainAuthority").val()) > 0)
		{
			params += '&params[lowerLimitDomainAuthority]=' + Math.round($("#lowerLimitDomainAuthority").val());
		}

		if(Math.round($("#upperLimitMozDomains").val()) < 10 && Math.round($("#upperLimitMozDomains").val()) >= 0)
		{
			if($("#upperLimitMozDomains").val() != '')
				params += '&params[upperLimitMozDomains]=' + Math.round($("#upperLimitMozDomains").val());
		}
		if(Math.round($("#lowerLimitMozDomains").val()) > 0)
		{
			params += '&params[lowerLimitMozDomains]=' + Math.round($("#lowerLimitMozDomains").val());
		}

		if(Math.round($("#upperLimitMozSubDomainDomains").val()) < 10 && Math.round($("#upperLimitMozSubDomainDomains").val()) >= 0)
		{
			if($("#upperLimitMozSubDomainDomains").val() != '')
				params += '&params[upperLimitMozSubDomainDomains]=' + Math.round($("#upperLimitMozSubDomainDomains").val());
		}

		if(Math.round($("#lowerLimitMozSubDomainDomains").val()) > 0)
		{
			params += '&params[lowerLimitMozSubDomainDomains]=' + Math.round($("#lowerLimitMozSubDomainDomains").val());
		}

		if(Math.round($("#upperLimitCitationFlow").val()) < 100 && Math.round($("#upperLimitCitationFlow").val()) >= 0)
		{
			if($("#upperLimitCitationFlow").val() != '')
				params += '&params[upperLimitCitationFlow]=' + Math.round($("#upperLimitCitationFlow").val());
		}
		if(Math.round($("#lowerLimitCitationFlow").val()) > 0)
		{
			params += '&params[lowerLimitCitationFlow]=' + Math.round($("#lowerLimitCitationFlow").val());
		}

		if(Math.round($("#upperLimitTrustFlow").val()) < 100 && Math.round($("#upperLimitTrustFlow").val()) >= 0)
		{
			if($("#upperLimitTrustFlow").val() != '')
				params += '&params[upperLimitTrustFlow]=' + Math.round($("#upperLimitTrustFlow").val());
		}
		if(Math.round($("#lowerLimitTrustFlow").val()) > 0)
		{
			params += '&params[lowerLimitTrustFlow]=' + Math.round($("#lowerLimitTrustFlow").val());
		}

		if($("#upperLimitTFCFRatio").val() < 5 && $("#upperLimitTFCFRatio").val() >= 0)
		{
			if($("#upperLimitTFCFRatio").val() != '')
				params += '&params[upperLimitTFCFRatio]=' + $("#upperLimitTFCFRatio").val();
		}
		if($("#lowerLimitTFCFRatio").val() > 0)
		{
			params += '&params[lowerLimitTFCFRatio]=' + $("#lowerLimitTFCFRatio").val();
		}

		if(Math.round($("#upperLimitTopicalTrustFlow").val()) < 100 && Math.round($("#upperLimitTopicalTrustFlow").val()) >= 0)
		{
			if($("#upperLimitTopicalTrustFlow").val() != '')
				params += '&params[upperLimitTopicalTrustFlow]=' + Math.round($("#upperLimitTopicalTrustFlow").val());
		}
		if(Math.round($("#lowerLimitTopicalTrustFlow").val()) > 0)
		{
			params += '&params[lowerLimitTopicalTrustFlow]=' + Math.round($("#lowerLimitTopicalTrustFlow").val());
		}


		if(Math.round($('#upperLimitPrice').val()) >= 0 && Math.round($('#upperLimitPrice').val()) < 100000)
		{
			if(Math.round($('#upperLimitPrice').val()) >= 1 && Math.round($('#upperLimitPrice').val()) <= 9){
				var sliderDomainVal = 1;
			}
			else if(Math.round($('#upperLimitPrice').val()) >= 10 && Math.round($('#upperLimitPrice').val()) <= 19){
				var sliderDomainVal = 2;
			}
			else if(Math.round($('#upperLimitPrice').val()) >= 20 && Math.round($('#upperLimitPrice').val()) <= 49){
				var sliderDomainVal = 3;
			}
			else if(Math.round($('#upperLimitPrice').val()) >= 50 && Math.round($('#upperLimitPrice').val()) <= 99){
				var sliderDomainVal = 4;
			}
			else if(Math.round($('#upperLimitPrice').val()) >= 100 && Math.round($('#upperLimitPrice').val()) <= 199){
				var sliderDomainVal = 5;
			}
			else if(Math.round($('#upperLimitPrice').val()) >= 200 && Math.round($('#upperLimitPrice').val()) <= 499){
				var sliderDomainVal = 6;
			}
			else if(Math.round($('#upperLimitPrice').val()) >= 500 && Math.round($('#upperLimitPrice').val()) <= 999){
				var sliderDomainVal = 7;
			}
			else if(Math.round($('#upperLimitPrice').val()) >= 1000 && Math.round($('#upperLimitPrice').val()) <= 1999){
				var sliderDomainVal = 8;
			}
			else if(Math.round($('#upperLimitPrice').val()) >= 2000 && Math.round($('#upperLimitPrice').val()) <= 4999){
				var sliderDomainVal = 9;
			}
			else if(Math.round($('#upperLimitPrice').val()) >= 5000){
				var sliderDomainVal = 10;
			}
			if($("#upperLimitPrice").val() != ''){
				params += '&params[upperLimitDomainPrice]=' + sliderDomainVal;
				params += '&params[upperLimitPrice]=' + Math.round($('#upperLimitPrice').val());
			}
		}
		if(Math.round($('#lowerLimitPrice').val()) > 0)
		{
			if(Math.round($('#lowerLimitPrice').val()) >= 1 && Math.round($('#lowerLimitPrice').val()) <= 9){
				var sliderDomainVal = 1;
			}
			else if(Math.round($('#lowerLimitPrice').val()) >= 10 && Math.round($('#lowerLimitPrice').val()) <= 19){
				var sliderDomainVal = 2;
			}
			else if(Math.round($('#lowerLimitPrice').val()) >= 20 && Math.round($('#lowerLimitPrice').val()) <= 49){
				var sliderDomainVal = 3;
			}
			else if(Math.round($('#lowerLimitPrice').val()) >= 50 && Math.round($('#lowerLimitPrice').val()) <= 99){
				var sliderDomainVal = 4;
			}
			else if(Math.round($('#lowerLimitPrice').val()) >= 100 && Math.round($('#lowerLimitPrice').val()) <= 199){
				var sliderDomainVal = 5;
			}
			else if(Math.round($('#lowerLimitPrice').val()) >= 200 && Math.round($('#lowerLimitPrice').val()) <= 499){
				var sliderDomainVal = 6;
			}
			else if(Math.round($('#lowerLimitPrice').val()) >= 500 && Math.round($('#lowerLimitPrice').val()) <= 999){
				var sliderDomainVal = 7;
			}
			else if(Math.round($('#lowerLimitPrice').val()) >= 1000 && Math.round($('#lowerLimitPrice').val()) <= 1999){
				var sliderDomainVal = 8;
			}
			else if(Math.round($('#lowerLimitPrice').val()) >= 2000 && Math.round($('#lowerLimitPrice').val()) <= 4999){
				var sliderDomainVal = 9;
			}
			else if(Math.round($('#lowerLimitPrice').val()) >= 5000){
				var sliderDomainVal = 10;
			}
			params += '&params[lowerLimitDomainPrice]=' + sliderDomainVal;
			params += '&params[lowerLimitPrice]=' + Math.round($('#lowerLimitPrice').val());
		}

		if(Math.round($('#upperLimitCtf').val()) >= 0 && Math.round($('#upperLimitCtf').val()) < 100000000)
		{
			if($("#upperLimitCtf").val() != '')
				params += '&params[upperLimitCtf]=' + Math.round($('#upperLimitCtf').val());
		}
		if(Math.round($('#lowerLimitCtf').val()) > 0)
		{
			params += '&params[lowerLimitCtf]=' + Math.round($('#lowerLimitCtf').val());
		}


		//Reintroduce Ahrefs metrics  - Picked from revision 75


		if(Math.round($('#upperLimitAhrefsDR').val()) >= 0 && Math.round($('#upperLimitAhrefsDR').val()) < 100)
		{
			if($("#upperLimitAhrefsDR").val() != '')
				params += '&params[upperLimitAhrefsDR]=' + Math.round($('#upperLimitAhrefsDR').val());
		}
		if(Math.round($('#lowerLimitAhrefsDR').val()) > 0)
		{
			params += '&params[lowerLimitAhrefsDR]=' + Math.round($('#lowerLimitAhrefsDR').val());
		}

		params += '&params[chkShowExtension_misc]=' + $("#chkShowExtension_misc").is(':checked');

		
				
			params += '&params[chkSaleTypeAuctions]=' + $("#chkSaleTypeAuctions").is(':checked');
			params += '&params[chkSaleTypeBuyNow]=' + $("#chkSaleTypeBuyNow").is(':checked');

			params += '&params[chkShowTypeGodaddy]=' + $("#chkShowTypeGodaddy").is(':checked');
			params += '&params[chkShowTypeNameJet]=' + $("#chkShowTypeNameJet").is(':checked');
			params += '&params[chkShowTypeSnapNames]=' + $("#chkShowTypeSnapNames").is(':checked');

			params += '&params[chkShowTypeDynaDot]=' + $("#chkShowTypeDynaDot").is(':checked');
			//params += '&params[chkShowTypeDropLists]=' + $("#chkShowTypeDropLists").is(':checked');
			params += '&params[chkShowTypeNameSilo]=' + $("#chkShowTypeNameSilo").is(':checked');

	return params;
}

function toggleFavorites(domain)
{
	
	//if user is logged in  - else send him to register page
		
	//using ajax add domain to watchlist or remove it from watchlist
	$.ajaxSetup ({cache: false});
	//based on whats returned from php page - set image as disabled or enabled
	$.ajax({url:"https://www.domcop.com/service/favorites.php?dataSource=live&domain=" + domain, success:function(result){

	var watchlistIcon = document.getElementById("fav-" + domain);

	if(String(result).trim() == 'added')
	{
	  $(watchlistIcon).removeClass("icon-star-empty").addClass("icon-star");
	}
	else
	if(String(result).trim() == 'deleted')
	{
	  $(watchlistIcon).removeClass("icon-star").addClass("icon-star-empty");
	}

	}});
	
		
}


function excludeDomain(domain)
{
	
	//if user is logged in  - else send him to register page
		
	//using ajax add domain to watchlist or remove it from watchlist
	$.ajaxSetup ({cache: false});
	//based on whats returned from php page - set image as disabled or enabled
	$.ajax({url:"https://www.domcop.com/service/excludeDomain.php?dataSource=live&domain=" + domain, success:function(result){
	var watchlistIcon = document.getElementById("exc-" + domain);

	if(String(result).trim() == 'excluded')
	{
	  $(watchlistIcon).addClass("red");
	}

	}});
	
		
}

function ExportData()
{
	var totalRecords = $('#totalRecords').text();
	var limitCount = $('#limitCount').text();
	var oTable = $('#domcop-table').dataTable();
	var sortParam = oTable.fnSettings().aaSorting.toString();
        sortParam = sortParam.replace(",", "|").replace(",", "|").replace(",", "|");
	
	document.location = 'https://www.domcop.com/export' + '?mode=add&dataSource=live&searchMode=advanced&comSearch=&total=' + totalRecords + '&limitCount=' + limitCount + '&sort=' + sortParam + '&sid=18642';
	
}

function ShowOnlyAvailableDomains()
{
	
					$('input[name=chkRequireDomainAvailable]').attr('checked', true);
				RefreshTable();
		$('#ShowAvailableExpiredDomains').hide();
		$('#ShowAllExpiredDomains').show();
		
}

function ShowAllExpiredDomains()
{
	
					$('input[name=chkRequireDomainAvailable]').attr('checked', false);
				RefreshTable();
		$('#ShowAllExpiredDomains').hide();
		$('#ShowAvailableExpiredDomains').show();
		
}



    function ExecuteSavedSearch(x)
    {

	
		
	if(x == 'save')
	{
		if(!confirm('This will save a new search. If you would like to modify the existing search, please click "Cancel" and click on the "Modify Search" button, else click "OK"'))
		{
			return false;
		}
	}
	
		
	if(x == 'save' || x == 'modify')
	{
	
		var url = 'https://www.domcop.com/search?type=' + x + '&dataSource=live';
		if(x == 'modify') url = url + '&sid=18642';
		url = url + '&mode=' + $('#searchMode').val();
		var searchParams = GetSearchParams();
		searchParams = searchParams.replace(/params\[/g, "");
		searchParams =  searchParams.replace(/\]/g, "");
		createCookie("SrchPrmsCk",searchParams,365);
	
	      $.colorbox({href:url, maxWidth:"100%"});
		return false;
	}
	else
	{
		document.location = 'https://www.domcop.com/?sid=' + x;
	}

    }

    function DeleteSearch()
    {
	if(confirm('Are you sure you want to delete this search?'))
	{
		
		document.location = 'https://www.domcop.com/search?action=delete&sid=18642';
		
	}
    }

    function showAllFilter(){
    	
    	var url = 'https://www.domcop.com/showAllFilter';
    	url = url + '?dataSource=live&mode=' + $('#searchMode').val();
    	
    	$.colorbox({href:url, width:"80%"});
	    //$.colorbox({href:url, maxWidth:"100%"});
		return false;
    }


</script>
